Fox was also to retain theatrical, nontheatrical, and home video rights worldwide for the franchise's five subsequent films, which Lucasfilm produced and financed independently, through [May](/wiki/May "May") [2020](/wiki/2020 "2020"), at which time ownership was to transfer to Disney. This complex relationship between Fox and Disney, particularly in regards to Fox's perpetual rights to Episode IV, was to create an obstacle for any future boxed set comprising all nine films.[[14]](#cite_note-14) On [December 14](/wiki/December_14 "December 14"), [2017](/wiki/2017 "2017"), The Walt Disney Company announced that it was acquiring most of Fox's parent company, [21st Century Fox](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/21st_Century_Fox "wikipedia:21st Century Fox"), including the film studio and all distribution rights to *A New Hope*.[[15]](#cite_note-Acquire-15) On [March 20](/wiki/March_20 "March 20"), [2019](/wiki/2019 "2019"), the [deal](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Acquisition_of_21st_Century_Fox_by_Disney "wikipedia:Acquisition of 21st Century Fox by Disney") was officially completed.[[16]](#cite_note-16) On [April 12](/wiki/April_12 "April 12"), 2019, a [Blu-ray](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Blu-ray "wikipedia:Blu-ray") box set containing the nine main installments of the *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* [saga](/wiki/Star_Wars_saga "Star Wars saga") remastered in 4K was reportedly announced to be in development for a [2020](/wiki/2020 "2020") release.[[17]](#cite_note-17)

## Reception ‡

In interviews, George Lucas said that George Bush was not an influence in writing the movie. Rather, he wrote the basic story outline in the 1970s during the Vietnam War, thinking of President Richard Nixon.[[18]](#cite_note-18) He stated at Cannes, "The parallels between what we did in Vietnam and what we're doing in Iraq now are unbelievable."[[19]](#cite_note-19) Lucas added that in more general terms, his story represents how any democracy can turn into a dictatorship with the consent of the people, like Caesar of Rome and Napoleon I of France.[[20]](#cite_note-20)[[21]](#cite_note-21)

### Popular reception

In the era of the internet, *Revenge of the Sith* has proven to be a major source for content in internet meme culture. In particular, Kenobi's greeting to Grievous on Utapau, "[hello there](/wiki/Hello_there "Hello there")," has arisen to one of the most famous *Star Wars* memes[[22]](#cite_note-Screen_Rant_article-22) and has been referenced in official works,[[23]](#cite_note-ObiWan5-23)[[24]](#cite_note-AgeofRepub-24) even being included as Kenobi's greeting to Luke Skywalker within the *[Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Star Wars: Obi-Wan Kenobi")* [Disney+](/wiki/Disney%2B "Disney+") series, where Ewan McGregor and Hayden Christensen reprised their roles as Kenobi and Vader, respectively.[[25]](#cite_note-Part_VI-25)

## Deleted scenes ‡

Six deleted scenes were included on Disc 2 of the DVD:

* "Grievous Slaughters Shaak Ti" - The death of [Shaak Ti](/wiki/Shaak_Ti/Legends "Shaak Ti/Legends") by [General](/wiki/General "General") [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous") on board the [*Invisible Hand*](/wiki/Invisible_Hand/Legends "Invisible Hand/Legends"). Deleted due to time constraints, and because the story was changed that Grievous left Shaak Ti on Coruscant alive, and she didn't die.
* "A Stirring in the Senate" - The First Meeting of the [Rebel Alliance](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic/Legends "Alliance to Restore the Republic/Legends"). Deleted because it took away from the central plot of Anakin Skywalker.
* "Seeds of Rebellion" - The Second Meeting of the Rebel Alliance. Deleted because it took away from the central plot of Anakin Skywalker.
* "Confronting the Chancellor" - The Presentation of the [Delegation of 2000](/wiki/Delegation_of_2000 "Delegation of 2000") to [Palpatine](/wiki/Palpatine/Legends "Palpatine/Legends"). Deleted because it took away from the central plot of Anakin Skywalker.
* "A Plot to Destroy the Jedi?" - [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu/Legends "Mace Windu/Legends") senses the destruction of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order/Legends "Jedi Order/Legends"). Deleted due to time constraints and because the point was already known.
* "Exiled to Dagobah" - Yoda lands on [Dagobah](/wiki/Dagobah/Legends "Dagobah/Legends"). Deleted for fear it would clutter up the endings instead of making it just "father, mother, and the kids." Rick McCallum is quoted as saying that this was the biggest loss for him to the film and he hopes to see it on a future edition.

Other scenes were also cut from the film:

* [Obi-Wan](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi/Legends "Obi-Wan Kenobi/Legends") visits Senator Amidala to discuss [Anakin](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker/Legends "Anakin Skywalker/Legends"), and tell her that he knows of her marriage. This scene features in the script, novel and comic book adaptation of the film, albeit differing slightly in each.
* Obi-Wan selects [Boga](/wiki/Boga/Legends "Boga/Legends") from the other [varactyls](/wiki/Varactyl/Legends "Varactyl/Legends"). An animatic of this scene was put on [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") in November 2007.
* The Deaths of [Luminara Unduli](/wiki/Luminara_Unduli/Legends "Luminara Unduli/Legends") and [Barriss Offee](/wiki/Barriss_Offee/Legends "Barriss Offee/Legends"). This scene was never shot.
* The [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66/Legends "Order 66/Legends") "death" of [Quinlan Vos](/wiki/Quinlan_Vos/Legends "Quinlan Vos/Legends"). This scene was never shot.
* The Order 66 death of [Mina Podia](/wiki/Mina_Podia "Mina Podia"). This scene was never shot.
* Another death of [Shaak Ti](/wiki/Shaak_Ti/Legends "Shaak Ti/Legends"), elaborated in the novelization: Ti is stabbed in the back by Darth Vader during his raid on the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Jedi_Temple/Legends "Jedi Temple/Legends") while she is meditating. She asks Anakin what happened to Windu, [Fisto](/wiki/Kit_Fisto/Legends "Kit Fisto/Legends"), [Kolar](/wiki/Agen_Kolar/Legends "Agen Kolar/Legends"), and [Tiin](/wiki/Saesee_Tiin/Legends "Saesee Tiin/Legends"). Skywalker replies by stabbing her in the back (a similar death of Shaak Ti appeared in *[LEGO Star Wars: The Video Game](/wiki/LEGO_Star_Wars:_The_Video_Game "LEGO Star Wars: The Video Game")*).
* Obi-Wan eluding the [Nos monster](/wiki/Nos_monster/Legends "Nos monster/Legends"), a natural predator of [Utapau](/wiki/Utapau/Legends "Utapau/Legends"), after falling into the sinkhole on Utapau.
* Talk scenes between [Aayla Secura](/wiki/Aayla_Secura/Legends "Aayla Secura/Legends") and [Bly](/wiki/Bly/Legends "Bly/Legends"), and [Plo Koon](/wiki/Plo_Koon/Legends "Plo Koon/Legends") and [Jag](/wiki/Jai%27galaar_(clone) "Jai'galaar (clone)").
* An ambush scene by [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda/Legends "Yoda/Legends"), [Tarfful](/wiki/Tarfful/Legends "Tarfful/Legends"), and [Chewbacca](/wiki/Chewbacca/Legends "Chewbacca/Legends"). A Clone Walker passes by a lake. Tarfful is lying dead on Wookiee boat. The clone stares at him for a moment and a furry creature covered in mud all over comes out of the water onto the boat. The clone asks the creature if anything is there. "Wookiee good, eat Wookiee," replies the creature. The clone decides it is just a native [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk/Legends "Kashyyyk/Legends") creature and decides to leave. Immediately, Chewbacca jumps out of the water and pulls the clone underwater, killing him. Then Tarfful wakes up and the creature reveals itself to be Yoda. He tells the Wookiees to give him a second to bathe. Yoda jumps into the water and scrubs all the mud off. Yoda emerges and puts on his robes. They then continue towards the emergency escape pod.
* A scene in which Yoda speaks to the voice of [Qui-Gon Jinn's](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn/Legends "Qui-Gon Jinn/Legends") [spirit](/wiki/Force_ghost/Legends "Force ghost/Legends"). Yoda dedicates himself to Qui-Gon's teachings. This scene was featured in the [novelization](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Revenge_of_the_Sith_(novelization) "Star Wars: Revenge of the Sith (novelization)").
* Darth Vader kills [Wat Tambor](/wiki/Wat_Tambor/Legends "Wat Tambor/Legends").

|  |
| --- |
| * **[Aidan Barton](/wiki/Aidan_Barton "Aidan Barton")** as **[Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker")** and **[Princess Leia](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo")** * **[Jerome Blake](/wiki/Jerome_Blake "Jerome Blake")** as **[Mas Amedda](/wiki/Mas_Amedda "Mas Amedda")** * **[Ben Cooke](/wiki/Ben_Cooke "Ben Cooke")** as **[Kit Fisto](/wiki/Kit_Fisto "Kit Fisto")** * **[Fay David](/wiki/Fay_David "Fay David")** as **[Luminara Unduli](/wiki/Luminara_Unduli "Luminara Unduli")** * **[Mimi Daraphet](/wiki/Mimi_Daraphet "Mimi Daraphet")** as **[Bultar Swan](/wiki/Bultar_Swan "Bultar Swan")** * **[Chantal Freer](/wiki/Chantal_Freer "Chantal Freer")** as **[Ellé](/wiki/Ell%C3%A9 "Ellé")** * **[Nick Gillard](/wiki/Nick_Gillard "Nick Gillard")** as **[Cin Drallig](/wiki/Cin_Drallig "Cin Drallig")** * **[Pablo Hidalgo](/wiki/Pablo_Hidalgo "Pablo Hidalgo")** as **[Janu Godalhi](/wiki/Janu_Godalhi "Janu Godalhi")** * **[James Earl Jones](/wiki/James_Earl_Jones "James Earl Jones")** as the voice of **[Darth Vader](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker")** * **[Olive Levi](/wiki/Olive_Levi "Olive Levi")** as **[Fema Baab](/wiki/Fema_Baab "Fema Baab")** * **[Bai Ling](/wiki/Bai_Ling "Bai Ling")** as **[Bana Breemu](/wiki/Bana_Breemu "Bana Breemu")** * **[George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas")** as **[Papanoida](/wiki/Notluwiski_Papanoida "Notluwiski Papanoida")** * **[T.V. Moore](/wiki/T.V._Moore "T.V. Moore")** and **Dean Mitchell** as **[Cellheim Anujo](/wiki/Cellheim_Anujo "Cellheim Anujo")** * **[Lily Nyamwasa](/wiki/Lily_Nyamwasa "Lily Nyamwasa")** as **[Stass Allie](/wiki/Stass_Allie "Stass Allie")** * **[Jeremy Prestoe](/wiki/Jeremy_Prestoe "Jeremy Prestoe")** as **[Tundra Dowmeia](/wiki/Tundra_Dowmeia "Tundra Dowmeia")** * **[Orli Shoshan](/wiki/Orli_Shoshan "Orli Shoshan")** as **[Shaak Ti](/wiki/Shaak_Ti "Shaak Ti")** * **[Paul Spence](/wiki/Paul_Spence "Paul Spence")** as **[Ask Aak](/wiki/Ask_Aak "Ask Aak")**   [Most of the lead cast](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/SW3_Cast.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070324194457) [Most of the lead cast](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/SW3_Cast.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070324194457)   Most of the lead cast    [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas") makes a cameo appearance at the [Galaxies Opera House](/wiki/Galaxies_Opera_House/Legends "Galaxies Opera House/Legends"). He is the blue-faced being, named [Baron](/wiki/Baron "Baron") [Papanoida](/wiki/Notluwiski_Papanoida "Notluwiski Papanoida"), seen just outside Palpatine's private box. It marks Lucas's first and only appearance in any of the *Star Wars* films. His three children also have cameos: Jett as a young Jedi-in-training called [Zett Jukassa](/wiki/Zett_Jukassa "Zett Jukassa") at the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Jedi_Temple/Legends "Jedi Temple/Legends"), his daughter Amanda as a senator called [Terr Taneel](/wiki/Terr_Taneel "Terr Taneel"), and Katie as a blue-skinned alien senator called [Chi Eekway Papanoida](/wiki/Chi_Eekway_Papanoida "Chi Eekway Papanoida"), visible when Palpatine arrives at the Senate after being saved by the Jedi.  Much of the crew make cameos in the film. For example [Nick Gillard](/wiki/Nick_Gillard "Nick Gillard"), the stunt coordinator, plays a character named [Cin Drallig](/wiki/Cin_Drallig "Cin Drallig") (his name spelled backwards, omitting the *k*). [Rick McCallum](/wiki/Rick_McCallum "Rick McCallum")'s daughter [Mousy](/wiki/Mousy_McCallum "Mousy McCallum") plays one of the Padawans killed by Darth Vader, named [Bene](/wiki/Bene "Bene"). Visual effects supervisor [John Knoll](/wiki/John_Knoll "John Knoll") played the Coruscant firefighter pilot. When Palpatine, Anakin, and Obi-Wan are falling down the elevator shaft in the beginning of the movie, it is John Knoll's hand that grabs the wire, not [Hayden Christensen](/wiki/Hayden_Christensen "Hayden Christensen")'s. Also in the movie was [Jeremy Bulloch](/wiki/Jeremy_Bulloch "Jeremy Bulloch") ([Boba Fett](/wiki/Boba_Fett "Boba Fett") in the [original trilogy](/wiki/Original_trilogy "Original trilogy")), who played [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Jeremoch Colton](/wiki/Jeremoch_Colton "Jeremoch Colton"), the pilot of the [CR70 corvette](/wiki/CR70_corvette/Legends "CR70 corvette/Legends"), and later CR90 Rebel Blockade Runner, *[Tantive III](/wiki/Tantive_III "Tantive III")*. This was a speaking role. A number of Lucasfilm and ILM employees also made cameo appearances on the balconies of the Galaxies Opera House, while on the steps [Anthony Daniels](/wiki/Anthony_Daniels "Anthony Daniels") reprised his Episode II cameo as [Dannl Faytonni](/wiki/Dannl_Faytonni "Dannl Faytonni"). |
